$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Do_While_Loops_Printing1

::Do While Loops Level 1 #000::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int d = 82;
do
\{
	cout << d << " ";
	d = d - 10;
\} while (d > 42);
	{
	=82 72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 42 
	~82 72 62 
	~82 72 62 52 42 
	}

::Do While Loops Level 1 #001::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int h = 3;
do
\{
	cout << h << " ";
	h = h + 1;
\} while (h <= 7);
	{
	=3 4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 8 
	~3 4 5 6 
	~3 4 5 6 7 8 
	}

<pre>int g = 2767;
do
\{

	{
	=2767 276 27 2 
	~276 27 2 
	~276 27 2 0 
	~2767 276 27 
	~2767 276 27 2 0 
	}

::Do While Loops Level 3 #500::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>int i = 5;
do
\{
	int j = 7;
	do
	\{		cout << '*' << " ";
		j = j + 1;
	\} while (j < 10);
	i = i - 1;
\} while (i >= 3);
</pre>	{
	=9
	~4
	~3
	~12
	~16
	}

::Do While Loops Level 3 #501::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>int i = 16;
do
\{
	int j = 22;
	do
	\{		cout << '*' << " ";
		j = j - 5;
	\} while (j > 7);

do
\{
	int j = 42;
	do
	\{		cout << '*' << " ";
		j = j + 5;
	\} while (j <= 57);
	i = i - 1;
\} while (i >= 5);
</pre>	{
	=16
	~5
	~4
	~20
	~25
	}
